### 8. Core Data Parameters

This section contains the comprehensive list of all individual data parameters used in project files, translated into a consistent `camelCase` format for the API schema.

| Original Key   | Generated camelCase Name                            | Full Name                                                                          | Type            | Unit (SI / IP)                  | Description / Validation                                                                                              |
|:-------------- |:--------------------------------------------------- |:---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |:--------------- |:------------------------------- |:--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `undef`        | `undefined`                                         |                                                                                    | String          | -                               | Represents an undefined value.                                                                                        |
| `nodef`        | `notDefined`                                        | Not defined                                                                        | String          | -                               | Represents a 'not defined' state.                                                                                     |

Of course. I will now provide the next set of parameters, continuing with the same rigorous and consistent naming architecture.

This concludes the second block of 250 parameters. Please let me know when you are ready for the next 250 entries.





Of course. Here is the third block of parameters, continuing with the same rigorous and consistent naming architecture.

This section contains entries 501 through 750 of the "Core Data Parameters" section.
